# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-30 01:39:16.026666

### Base Program

```py
def count_vowel_strings(n):
    dp = [1, 1, 1, 1, 1]

    for i in range(1, n):
        for j in range(3, -1, -1):
            dp[j] += dp[j + 1]

    return sum(dp)
```

### Input

```json
[8]
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py
def count_vowel_strings(n):
    dp = [1, 1, 1, 1, 1]
    for i in range(1, n):
        for j in range(3, -1, -1):
            dp[j] += dp[j + 1]
    return sum(dp)
```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py
def count_vowel_strings(var_0):
    dp = [1, 1, 1, 1, 1]
    for i in range(1, var_0):
        for j in range(3, -1, -1):
            dp[j] += dp[j + 1]
    return sum(dp)
```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py
def count_vowel_strings(n):
    dp = [1, 1, 1, 1, 1]
    for i in range(1, n):
        for j in range(3, -1, -1):
            dp[j] += dp[1 + j]
    return sum(dp)
```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py
def count_vowel_strings(var_1):
    dp = [1, 1, 1, 1, 1]
    for i in range(1, var_1):
        for j in range(3, -1, -1):
            dp[j] += dp[1 + j]
    return sum(dp)
```
